        <h4 style="text-align:center;">
         Social Hub
        </h4>
        <h5 style="color:darkred; text-align:center;">
         #GimsSwiss
        </h5>
        <div id="container-social-wall">
        </div>
        <script>
         var init_sw_timer = 0;
    var sw_timer = 0;
    var sw_target = null;
    var scroll_sw = 0;
    function hideSocialWall(){
        $("#social-row").hide();
        $("#container-social-wall").hide();
            }
    function transformSocialPost(content){
        $(".social-element > .descr").markRegExp(/([@]|[#])([a-z])\w+/gmi);
    }
    function displaySocialWall(){
        var url_service = "https://socialhub.gims.swiss/";
        var url = "/fr/get-social-posts/";
        var error = true;
        $.ajax({
            url: url,
            type: "json",
            method: "POST",
            success: function(){
                error = false;
            },
            error: function(){
                error = true;
            }
        }).done(function(response){
                        if(error){
                hideSocialWall();
            }
            else if(typeof response.error != 'undefined' &&  response.error == true){
                hideSocialWall();
            }
            else{
                // go and display
                for(var i in response.posts){
                    var post = response.posts[i];

                    var div = document.createElement("div");

                    div.setAttribute("data-id", post.id);
                    var type = null;
                    if(post.post_video == null){
                        if(post.post_description==null){
                            var type = "image";
                        }
                        else{
                            var type = "image-with-text";
                        }
                    }
                    else{
                        var type = "video";
                    }
                    div.className = "social-element "+type;
                    div.setAttribute("data-descr","socialelement_"+i);
                    var header_div = document.createElement("div");

                    var fa_icon = "";
                    if(post.post_url.indexOf("facebook.com")!=-1){fa_icon = "fa-facebook";}
                    if(post.post_url.indexOf("instagram.com")!=-1){fa_icon = "fa-instagram";}
                    if(post.post_url.indexOf("google.com")!=-1){fa_icon = "fa-google";}
                    if(post.post_url.indexOf("twitter.com")!=-1){fa_icon = "fa-twitter";}

                    if(post.user_picture!=null && post.user_name!=null){
                        header_div.innerHTML = '<img src="'+post.user_picture+'"><span class="">@'+post.user_name+'</span><i class="fa '+fa_icon+'""></i>';
                    }
                    else{
                        header_div.innerHTML = '<i class="fa '+fa_icon+'"></i>';
                    }

                    header_div.className = "header-social-post";
                    header_div.id = "header_social_"+post.id;
                    div.appendChild(header_div);

                    var descr_div = document.createElement("div");
                    descr_div.innerHTML = post.post_description;
                    descr_div.className = "descr";
                    descr_div.id = "descr_"+post.id;


                    div.setAttribute('data-descr',"#descr_"+post.id);

                    if(typeof post.post_image_thumb!='undefined' && post.post_image_thumb != null && post.post_image_thumb!=""){
                        div.setAttribute('style','background-image:url(\''+post.post_image_thumb+'\');')
                        div.setAttribute('data-bg','background-image:url(\''+post.post_image_thumb+'\');')
                    }
                    else{
                        descr_div.style.display = "block";
                        descr_div.setAttribute('data-always', true);
                    }
                    div.appendChild(descr_div);

                    var link_post = document.createElement("a");

                    var link_url_post = post.platform_url;
                    link_post.setAttribute("href", url_service+link_url_post);
                    link_post.setAttribute("target","_blank");
                    link_post.appendChild(div);

                    var target_dest = document.getElementById('container-social-wall');
                    target_dest.appendChild(link_post);
                }

                transformSocialPost();
            }




            $(".social-element").on("mouseover", function(){

                if(init_sw_timer==0){
                    init_sw_timer = new Date();
                }

                sw_timer = setInterval(scrollSWElement,450);

                var descr = $(this).data("descr");
                if($(this).css('background-image')==""){
                    $(descr).show();
                }
            });

            $(".social-element").on("mouseover", function(){
                sw_target = $(this).data('descr');
                var descr = $(this).data("descr");
                if($(descr).html()!=""){
                    $(this).attr("style", "background-color:#48494B; background-image:none;");
                    $(descr).show();
                }
            });

            $(".social-element").on("mouseout", function(){
                var bg = $(this).data("bg");
                $(this).attr("style", bg);
                var descr = $(this).data("descr");
                if($(descr).data("always")!=true){
                    $(descr).hide();
                }
                else{

                }
                var myElement = document.getElementById(descr.replace("#",""));
                myElement.offsetTop = 0;
                init_sw_timer = 0;
                sw_timer = null;
                $(sw_target).scrollTop(0);
                sw_target = null;
                scroll_sw = 0;

            });
        });
    }

    function scrollSWElement(){
        var now = new Date();
        if(init_sw_timer!=0){
            var difference = (now - init_sw_timer) / 1000;

            if(difference>2){
                scroll_sw = scroll_sw + 1;
                $(sw_target).scrollTop(scroll_sw);
            }

        }
    }
        </script>
       </div>
      </div>
     </main>

  <script>
   var start_slide = null;
    var end_slide = null;
    var link_slide = null;
    var counter_click_slide = 0;

    var start_slide_p = null;
    var end_slide_p = null;
    var link_slide_p = null;
    var counter_click_slide_p = 0;

    var sliderHomeO = null;

    function checkIfSliding(){

        $("#slider2018-home-exposants").parent().each(function(){
            end_slide = bxslider.getCurrentSlide();
        });

        counter_click_slide++;
        if(counter_click_slide==1 && start_slide==end_slide && link_slide!=null){
            document.location.href=link_slide;
        }
        if(counter_click_slide>1){
            counter_click_slide=0;
        }

        return false;
    }

    function checkIfSlidingPremiers(){

        $("#slider2018-home-premiers").parent().each(function(){
            end_slide_p = bxslider_premiers.getCurrentSlide();
        });
        counter_click_slide_p++;
        if(counter_click_slide_p==1 && start_slide_p==end_slide_p && link_slide_p!=null){
            document.location.href=link_slide_p;
        }
        if(counter_click_slide_p>1){
            counter_click_slide_p=0;
        }

        return false;
    }

    $(".img-slide-premier").parent().on("mouseover", function(){
        var bgspan = $(this).data("bgspan");
        var span = $(this).data("span");
        var img = $(this).data("img");
        $(bgspan).show().css("display","block");
        $(span).show().css("display","block");
    });

    $(".img-slide-premier").parent().on("mouseout", function(){
        var bgspan = $(this).data("bgspan");
        var span = $(this).data("span");
        var img = $(this).data("img");
        $(bgspan).hide();
        $(span).hide();
    });

    $("#slider2018-home-exhibitors .slide-bx-link").on("mouseover",function(ev){
        start_slide = bxslider.getCurrentSlide();
        link_slide = $(this).data('link');
    });

    $("#slider2018-home-exhibitors .slide-bx-link").on("click",function(ev){
        setTimeout(checkIfSliding,100);
        ev.preventDefault();
    });

    $("#slider2018-home-premiers .slide-bx-link").on("mouseover",function(ev){

        start_slide_p = bxslider_premiers.getCurrentSlide();
        link_slide_p = $(this).data('link');
    });

    $("#slider2018-home-premiers .slide-bx-link").on("click",function(ev){
        ev.preventDefault();
        setTimeout(checkIfSlidingPremiers,100);
        ev.preventDefault();
    });
